## Frequently Asked Questions

### What is Vidfly's AI Video Generator?

Vidfly is an all-in-one AI video platform that lets you create videos from text, images, or AI avatars. It uses leading AI models to generate high-quality, cinematic content in just seconds.

### Can I generate videos without editing skills or filming?

Yes. Vidfly allows you to create complete videos using simple prompts or uploaded images. No shooting, scripting, or editing skills are required.

### What types of videos can I create with Vidfly?

You can create short videos, marketing content, AI avatars, product explainers, cinematic scenes, story animations, and more—powered by advanced text-to-video and image-to-video models.

### How fast is the Vidfly AI Video Generator?

Designed for speed, the Vidfly AI Video Generator can create videos much faster than most competitors. The exact time depends on the complexity of your input, your requirements, and the model you choose.

### Are there watermarks on videos or images generated by Vidfly AI?

If you're using Vidfly's free plan, your generated videos or images will include a watermark. To remove the watermark, you’ll need to upgrade to one of Vidfly’s paid subscription plans.

### Can I use Vidfly AI creations for commercial projects?

Yes. Subscribers on Vidfly's paid plans can use the videos or images they create for commercial purposes, including advertisements, marketing campaigns, product demos, and more.

### Is Vidfly AI free to try?

Absolutely! Vidfly offers a free plan so users can test its features and generate videos or images at no cost. Paid plans are available for those who need more credits, advanced tools, or enhanced capabilities.
